3+3x3+3+3 BIDMAS or BODMAS is used  B brackets I indices D division M multiplication A addition S subtraction To work this out,you need follow the order from B to S 3+3x3+3+3 Multiplication comes before Addition so we work out the multiplication which is 3x3=9 Now we do addition,3+3=6 and then you have the 3 at the start  So,3x3=9 and 3+3=6 so 9+6=15 Dont forget your 3 at the start so 15+3=18 SO THE ANSWER TO 3+3x3+3+3=18ğŸ˜Š (Hope That Helps!ğŸ˜Š)

The thing about roman numerals is that you kind of have to do addition to get the number, so in a way it is math with a mix of algebra if you see the symbols as variables with X's representing 10s, V's 5s, and I's representing numbers up to 3. If an I is placed before a symbol such as X or V it is considered subtracting from that amount, so IX would be 9 and IV would be 4. If it is placed after, it is considered to be adding to the symbol, so XI would be 11 and VI would be 6. So XXXVIII is 10+10+10+5+3 (or 8) which would be 38. In conclusion, the Romans were extra

Fun mathematical way to do the teeth question: Count from one of your backmost teeth to the nearest front tooth. Then multiply by 4 because thatâ€™s half of half of the amount of your teeth. gonna end up making a vid about this in a few minutes  3 + 3 x 3 - 3 + 3  lord please read this pls pls pls  tl;dr: possible answers are 18 and 12. (for those who didn't see the reply under courtreezy's comment)  there are two ways that i see to solve this. (honors math student here)   the first version is straight forward. 3 + 3 is 6.  6 x 3 is 18. 18 - 3 is 15. and 15 + 3 is 18 again. therefore a possible answer would be 18.  now let's try order of operations. the system for order of operations is PEMDAS order. (for multiplication and division/addition and subtraction, it could go either way since when you go from left to right, you do which you see first) Parentheses Exponents Multiplication Division Addition Subtraction.  3 x 3 is 9. 3 + 9 is 12. 12 - 3 is 9. and 9 + 3 is 12. so it could also be 12.
